<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>пасть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pastʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</p>
<ol><li>to fall, to drop
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давление.html>давле́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>воды́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>ду́ше</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:упасть.html>упа́ло</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Davlénije vodý v dúše <b>upálo</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Water pressure in the shower <b>dropped</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to sink, to decline</li></ol>

***упереть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:упереть.html>упере́ть</a> (10893)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переть.html>пере́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упереть.html>упере́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uperétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упирать.html>упира́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rest <i>(against)</i>, to set <i>(against)</i>, to lean <i>(against)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:упереть.html>упере́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шест.html>шест</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стена.html>сте́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uperétʹ</b> šest v sténu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to rest a pole against the wall</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:упереть.html>упере́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бок.html>бок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uperétʹ</b> rúku v bok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to place/put one's hand on one's hip</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to steal, to pilfer, to filch</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lay stress <i>(on)</i></li></ol>

***упереться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:упереться.html>упере́ться</a> (3843)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упереть.html>упере́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uperétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упереться.html>упере́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uperétʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упираться.html>упира́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rest <i>(against)</i>, to set <i>(against)</i></li>
<li>to jib, to balk, to refuse</li>
<li>to be hampered, to be held back, to hinge <i>(on)</i></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упереть.html>упере́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uperétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***упиваться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:упиваться.html>упива́ться</a> (15950)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упиться.html>упи́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">upítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упиваться.html>упива́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">upivátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упиться.html>упи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get drunk</li>
<li>to revel <i>(in)</i>, to be intoxicated <i>(by)</i>, to feast one's eyes <i>(upon)</i>, to gloat <i>(over)</i></li></ol>

***упирать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:упирать.html>упира́ть</a> (25017)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-пирать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-piratʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the latter being a variant of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переть.html>пере́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perétʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to move, to carry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упирать.html>упира́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">upirátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упереть.html>упере́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rest <i>(against)</i>, to set <i>(against)</i>, to lean <i>(against)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:упирать.html>упира́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шест.html>шест</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стена.html>сте́ну</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>upirátʹ</b> šest v stenu</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to rest a pole against the wall</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:упирать.html>упира́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бок.html>бок</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>upirátʹ</b> rúku v bok</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to place/put one's hand on one's hip</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to steal, to pilfer, to filch</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lay stress <i>(on)</i></li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упор.html>упо́р</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">upór</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***упираться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:упираться.html>упира́ться</a> (4269)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упирать.html>упира́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">upirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упираться.html>упира́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">upirátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упереться.html>упере́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rest <i>(against)</i>, to set <i>(against)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:упираться.html>упира́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:локоть.html>ло́ктем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стена.html>сте́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>upirátʹsja</b> lóktem v stenu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to set one's elbow against the wall, lean one's elbow against the wall</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:упираться.html>упира́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>нога́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>зе́млю</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>upirátʹsja</b> nogámi v zémlju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take a firm stand, dig one's heels in the ground</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:упираться.html>упира́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаза́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>upirátʹsja</b> glazámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">stare</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:упираться.html>упира́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рог.html>ро́гом</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:упираться.html>упира́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>рука́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>нога́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>upirátʹsja</b> rógom, <b>upirátʹsja</b> rukámi i nogámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">be dead set <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">against</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, run one's head <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">against</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to jib, to balk, to refuse</li>
<li>to be hampered, to be held back, to hinge <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">on</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:решение.html>реше́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́са</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:упираться.html>упира́ется</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:недостаток.html>недоста́ток</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rešénije voprósa <b>upirájetsja</b> v nedostátok vrémeni</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">progress on the issue is being hampered by the lack of time</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:упираться.html>упира́ется</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:решение.html>реше́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:начальник.html>нача́льника</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vsjó <b>upirájetsja</b> v rešénije načálʹnika</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">everything hinges on the boss's decision</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упирать.html>упира́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">upirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:упирающий.html>упира́ющий</a> (25017)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<hr><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><i>действ. прич. <a href = vnd.unilang:наст.html>наст</a>. вр.</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:упирать.html>упира́ть</a> <span class="example-fullblock example-absent-block"><ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:платить.html>плати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">platítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***уплаченный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уплатить.html>упла́ченный</a> (12258)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уплатить.html>упла́ченный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">upláčennyj</span>)
</p>

***уплотнение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уплотнение.html>уплотне́ние</a> (19936)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уплотнение.html>уплотне́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uplotnénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уплотнение.html>уплотне́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уплотнение.html>уплотне́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уплотнение.html>уплотне́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>compaction, consolidation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:уплотнение.html>уплотне́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:линия.html>ли́нии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:связь.html>свя́зи</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uplotnénije</b> línii svjázi</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">multiplexing; multichannel operation</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>packing, sealing, gasketing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:уплотнение.html>уплотне́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стык.html>сты́ков</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uplotnénije</b> stýkov</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">joint packing</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:уплотнение.html>уплотне́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:трубный.html>тру́бных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:соединение.html>соедине́ний</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uplotnénije</b> trúbnyx sojedinénij</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">pipe sealing</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>gasket, packing, seal</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> infiltration, hardening</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">уплотнять</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uplotnjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уплотнить.html>уплотни́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uplotnitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уплыть.html>уплы́ть</a> (12749)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плыть.html>плы́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уплыть.html>уплы́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uplýtʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уплывать.html>уплыва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to swim away</li>
<li>to sail away</li></ol>

***уповать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уповать.html>упова́ть</a> (21992)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*upъvati</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">ufać</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уповать.html>упова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">upovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hope (for), to set one's hopes (upon) [+ <span><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span>(object)</span></span>] [+accusative]</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:упокой.html>упоко́й</a> (19938)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покой.html>поко́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упокой.html>упоко́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">upokój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упокой.html>упоко́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упокой.html>упоко́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упокой.html>упоко́ев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>repose, eternal rest <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a soul</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:упокой.html>упоко́й</a></strong></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">za upokój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">for the repose of <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">a soul; in a prayer</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
